# <a name="obsolete-types-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="49b5f-102">.NET Framework'teki eski türler</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49b5f-102">Obsolete Types in the .NET Framework</span></span>
<a name="introduction"></a> <span data-ttu-id="49b5f-103">Bu makaledeki tablolar, artık kullanılmayan türler listesinde [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] ve [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], derleme tarafından düzenlenmiş.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49b5f-103">The tables in this article list the types that are obsolete in the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] and the [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49b5f-104">Eski türler ve önerilen alternatifleri her derlemede bir listesini görmek için aşağıdaki bağlantıları kullanın.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49b5f-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete types and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49b5f-105">Bu tür geçersiz olduğundan, tüm üyeleri de artık kullanılmıyor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49b5f-105">Because these types are obsolete, all their members are also obsolete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49b5f-106">.NET Framework Sınıf Kitaplığı'nda ek eski üyeler listesi için bkz. [eski üyeler](obsolete-members.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49b5f-106">For a list of additional obsolete members in the .NET Framework class library, see [Obsolete Members](obsolete-members.md).</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="49b5f-925">Aşağıdaki bölümlerde, Microsoft derlemelerde eski türleri listelenmektedir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49b5f-925">The following sections list the obsolete types in Microsoft assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49b5f-926">Bu derlemeler, ayrı bir dil (örneğin, Microsoft.JScript.dll'ye veya Microsoft.VisualC.dll) hedef derlemeler gibi özel amaçlı derlemelerdir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49b5f-926">These assemblies are special-purpose assemblies such as assemblies that target an individual language (for example, Microsoft.JScript.dll or Microsoft.VisualC.dll).</span></span>

### <a name="assembly-iehostdll-and-ieexecexe"></a><span data-ttu-id="49b5f-927">Derleme: IEHost.dll ve IEExec.exe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49b5f-927">Assembly: IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="49b5f-928">IEHost.dll ve IEExec.exe derlemeler .NET Framework'den kaldırıldı.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49b5f-928">The IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe assemblies have been removed from the .NET Framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49b5f-929">Tüm türleri ve üyeleri artık kullanılmayan ve sürümünden desteklenmez [!INCLUDE[net_v40_short](../../../includes/net-v40-short-md.md)].</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49b5f-929">All of their types and their members are obsolete and are not supported as of the [!INCLUDE[net_v40_short](../../../includes/net-v40-short-md.md)].</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49b5f-930">Bu derlemeler, Internet Explorer'da yürütülebilir dosyaları çalışan ve Windows Forms denetimleri barındırmak için kullanıldı.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49b5f-930">These assemblies were used to host Windows Forms controls and to run executables in Internet Explorer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="49b5f-931">Önerilen alternatifler, ClickOnce, XAML tarayıcı uygulamaları (XBAP) içerir ve Microsoft Silverlight.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="49b5f-931">Recommended alternatives include ClickOnce, XAML browser applications (XBAP), and Microsoft Silverlight.</span></span>
